//　二人の自転車の音が聞こえなくなっても＠...俺はしばらくの間、二人を見送り続けていた￥
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺が、ぶっ飛ばしてやるからな。",
		   NULL, "I'll punch you right in the nose.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


	OutputLine(NULL, "　…その日まで、がんばろうな、沙都子。",
		   NULL, "...Let's try our best until that day comes, Satoko.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);


	OutputLine(NULL, "　二人の自転車の音が聞こえなくなっても。",
		   NULL, "Even if I could no longer hear the sounds of their bicycles.", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…俺はしばらくの間、二人を見送り続けていた。",
		   NULL, " ...I stood there for a while, seeing them off.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//■幕間

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering( 6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot( 7, "Title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
//	DrawBustshot( 5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
//	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );

	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask( "tata001", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 5000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawSceneWithMask( "black", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );



}
